79885 - ORE HISC-99 Fuel Loading Dock Hyper-Isomophic Strontium Clathrates refined to a 99% purity fuel is capable of liberating tremendous amounts of energy under controlled conditions, and can lead to catastrophe if mishandled. Although numerous safety measures are in place, in light of a number of early accidents with HISC refining involving spaceships, ORE makes it a rule to have vessels operating as interstellar supertankers arrive and take on their cargo at a special fuel loading dock placed some distance away from the Ice Refinery.

This dock is serviced by special Automated HISC-99 Tankers which ferry the refined fuel from the refinery to the loading dock under strict computer control. Any wayward tankers or those rescued from hijackers should be guided to this dock so the precious HISC-99 fuel can be offloaded securely.		 Guidance Objectives

79890 - ORE HISC-99 Ice Refinery As a key member of the Upwell Consortium, the Outer Ring Excavations (ORE) corporation has been keen to locate and exploit hidden reserves of rare ice containing valuable and rare deposits of Hyper-Isomorphic Strontium Clathrates (HISC). This rare, highly symmetrical, complex yet compact form of Strontium Clathrates is hard to extract and process but has high utility and value in the space industries. Much like standard Strontium Clathrates, HISC can be used to power structure defense systems and forcefields but with greater efficiency and theoretically much greater resistance to incoming damage.

Due to the rarity of the ice variants containing HISC (such as Geodesic Krystallos and Supersymmetrical Gelidus), and the extreme difficulty of processing the dense and molecularly complex ices into useful fuel, ORE has set up special central ice repository and refinery facilities in convenient ice fields. These facilities send out ice mining expeditions to seek more of the rare, fleeting fields of ice that contain the HISC-bearing ice variants and bring the raw materials back to the Ice Refinery for processing into the highly useful and extremely valuable HISC-99 fuel. To attain 99% purity, the raw HISC ices are cracked and refined in a special facility that pumps the high-value HISC-99 into special storage tanks.

The Ice Refinery controls a number of special Automated HISC-99 Tankers which ferry the refined fuel from the refinery to a remote spaceship loading dock under strict computer control. This safety precaution is designed to prevent any accidents involving spaceships that might lead to the catastrophic liberation of the tremendous amounts of energy that HISC-99 can unleash. 79909 - Automated HISC-99 Tanker Special Automated HISC-99 Tankers based on the Porpoise-class mining support vessel are used to ferry the valuable fuel from the Ice Refinery to the Fuel Loading dock. The safety precaution of having any interstellar supertanker vessel or other spaceship pick up cargo from a location some distance from the Ice Refinery is the result of early accidents involving the potent HISC-99 fuel, which is capable of liberating tremendous energies. The heavily-modified automated tankers have had their ore and fuel bays converted to hold the HISC-99 securely, and the vessels are equipped with prodigious shielding and heavy armor.

Although the Automated HISC-99 Tankers are under the central control of the Ice Refinery's guidance computers, it is possible for pirates to broadcast interference signals that jam the guidance commands and allow them to hack the onboard navigation systems. Pirates will seek to guide any hijacked tankers to their loading scaffold, where a modified freighter awaits the precious loot. As pirate forces and Upwell security struggle for control of the facility, any anti-pirate capsuleers can guide wayward tankers to the ORE HISC-99 Fuel Loading Dock.		 Guided Entities

While an assault on the Ice Refinery is impractical and would be likely to result in an explosion capable of destroying everything in the vicinity, the special Automated HISC-99 Tankers the facility uses to ferry the fuel to a loading dock can be hacked and hijacked without too much difficulty.

The pirates have a heavily-modified, suitably-shielded freighter on standby and are using this improvised scaffold to load the stolen HISC-99 fuel into their pirate supertanker. 699251 ORE HISC-99 Fuel Loading Dock ORE HISC-99 Fuel Loading Dock Name of item 79885 (Guidance Objectives)
699252 Hyper-Isomophic Strontium Clathrates refined to a 99% purity fuel is capable of liberating tremendous amounts of energy under controlled conditions, and can lead to catastrophe if mishandled. Although numerous safety measures are in place, in light of a number of early accidents with HISC refining involving spaceships, ORE makes it a rule to have vessels operating as interstellar supertankers arrive and take on their cargo at a special fuel loading dock placed some distance away from the Ice Refinery.

This dock is serviced by special Automated HISC-99 Tankers which ferry the refined fuel from the refinery to the loading dock under strict computer control. Any wayward tankers or those rescued from hijackers should be guided to this dock so the precious HISC-99 fuel can be offloaded securely. 699254 The Angel Cartel is attempting to steal the valuable HISC-99 fuel being refined by ORE at this location. While an assault on the Ice Refinery is impractical and would be likely to result in an explosion capable of destroying everything in the vicinity, the special Automated HISC-99 Tankers the facility uses to ferry the fuel to a loading dock can be hacked and hijacked without too much difficulty.

The pirates have a heavily-modified, suitably-shielded freighter on standby and are using this improvised scaffold to load the stolen HISC-99 fuel into their pirate supertanker. Any automated tankers hijacked by pirate capsuleers are to be guided to this location for pickup by the Angel Cartel. 706227 Special Automated HISC-99 Tankers based on the Porpoise-class mining support vessel are used to ferry the valuable fuel from the Ice Refinery to the Fuel Loading dock. The safety precaution of having any interstellar supertanker vessel or other spaceship pick up cargo from a location some distance from the Ice Refinery is the result of early accidents involving the potent HISC-99 fuel, which is capable of liberating tremendous energies. The heavily-modified automated tankers have had their ore and fuel bays converted to hold the HISC-99 securely, and the vessels are equipped with prodigious shielding and heavy armor.

Although the Automated HISC-99 Tankers are under the central control of the Ice Refinery's guidance computers, it is possible for pirates to broadcast interference signals that jam the guidance commands and allow them to hack the onboard navigation systems. Pirates will seek to guide any hijacked tankers to their loading scaffold, where a modified freighter awaits the precious loot. As pirate forces and Upwell security struggle for control of the facility, any anti-pirate capsuleers can guide wayward tankers to the ORE HISC-99 Fuel Loading Dock.		 Special Automated HISC-99 Tankers based on the <i>Porpoise</i>-class mining support vessel are used to ferry the valuable fuel from the Ice Refinery to the Fuel Loading dock. 706317 Ice Refinery Heist Ice Refinery Heist UI/Agency/PirateIncursions/Guides/Activities/IceRefineryHeistName
706318 5-30 5-30 UI/Agency/PirateIncursions/Guides/Activities/IceRefineryHeistActivityScaling
706319 During an Ice Refinery Heist pirate NPCs are in the process of hijacking automated fuel tankers carrying refined HISC-99 fuel. The precious fuel refined from rare ices must be recovered by empire militia pilots responding to ORE's call for help, or seized for the pirate cause by renegade capsuleers. The automated fuel tankers must be guided away from the central Ice Refinery structure to a secure ORE fuel loading dock, or to a loading scaffold set up by the pirates in order to steal the HISC-99 with modified pirate freighters.

Guidance can be initiated by interacting with an automated fuel tanker when within close range. The guidance connection with the automated tankers can be lost if the guiding ship gets too far away from it. The range at which a guidance connection can be maintained is somewhat greater than the close range at which guidance must be started.

When a capsuleer initiates guidance of an automated fuel tanker, it will automatically move towards the loading area of the faction the capsuleer is supporting, either the loading scaffold of the pirate faction raiding the refinery, or for empire militia pilots, the ORE loading dock. Once an automated tanker reaches the loading area safely it will be counted as a successful fuel recovery for the relevant side. The target for fuel recovery operations and the progress of each side towards it will be displayed when entering the activity site.		 During an Ice Refinery Heist pirate NPCs are in the process of hijacking automated fuel tankers carrying refined HISC-99 fuel. The precious fuel refined from rare ices must be recovered by empire militia pilots responding to ORE's call for help, or seized for the pirate cause by renegade capsuleers. The automated fuel tankers must be <b>guided</b> away from the central Ice Refinery structure to a secure ORE fuel loading dock, or to a loading scaffold set up by the pirates in order to steal the HISC-99 with modified pirate freighters.

<b>Guidance</b> can be initiated by interacting with an automated fuel tanker when within close range. The guidance connection with the automated tankers can be lost if the guiding ship gets too far away from it. The range at which a guidance connection can be maintained is somewhat greater than the close range at which guidance must be started.

When a capsuleer initiates <b>guidance</b> of an automated fuel tanker, it will automatically move towards the loading area of the faction the capsuleer is supporting, either the loading scaffold of the pirate faction raiding the refinery, or for empire militia pilots, the ORE loading dock. Once an automated tanker reaches the loading area safely it will be counted as a successful fuel recovery for the relevant side. The target for fuel recovery operations and the progress of each side towards it will be displayed when entering the activity site.		 UI/Agency/PirateIncursions/Guides/Activities/IceRefineryHeistHowTo
706320 Pilots will receive LP from their enlisted faction for successful completion of an Ice Refinery Heist activity. LP rewards will be evenly divided among all participants aligned to the winning faction who are present upon completion. Some of these sites may also include reward scaling, with an increasing total reward up to a certain number of pilots – this is indicated by the number included in the name of the site such as 'ADV-30', indicating the reward scales up to 30 pilots before individual payouts begin to decrease.

Completion of these activities will also contribute to the pilot’s individual contribution rewards pool. As the pilot generates corruption or suppression for their faction during insurgencies, additional LP and ISK rewards will be paid out upon completion of the insurgency, with larger rewards available to pilots aligned with the winning faction. 706321 Ice Refinery Heist activities can be found in systems which are in the third or fourth stage of either Suppression or Corruption. Once the fifth stage is reached ORE will have evacuated its processed fuel and refinery equipment from the system. Once the fifth stage is reached ORE will have evacuated its processed fuel and refinery equipment from the system. UI/Agency/PirateIncursions/Guides/Activities/IceRefineryHeistWhere
706330 As a key member of the Upwell Consortium, the Outer Ring Excavations (ORE) corporation has been keen to locate and exploit hidden reserves of rare ice containing valuable and rare deposits of Hyper-Isomorphic Strontium Clathrates (HISC). This rare, highly symmetrical, complex yet compact form of Strontium Clathrates is hard to extract and process but has high utility and value in the space industries. Much like standard Strontium Clathrates, HISC can be used to power structure defense systems and forcefields but with greater efficiency and theoretically much greater resistance to incoming damage.

Due to the rarity of the ice variants containing HISC (such as Geodesic Krystallos and Supersymmetrical Gelidus), and the extreme difficulty of processing the dense and molecularly complex ices into useful fuel, ORE has set up special central ice repository and refinery facilities in convenient ice fields. These facilities send out ice mining expeditions to seek more of the rare, fleeting fields of ice that contain the HISC-bearing ice variants and bring the raw materials back to the Ice Refinery for processing into the highly useful and extremely valuable HISC-99 fuel. To attain 99% purity, the raw HISC ices are cracked and refined in a special facility that pumps the high-value HISC-99 into special storage tanks.

The Ice Refinery controls a number of special Automated HISC-99 Tankers which ferry the refined fuel from the refinery to a remote spaceship loading dock under strict computer control. This safety precaution is designed to prevent any accidents involving spaceships that might lead to the catastrophic liberation of the tremendous amounts of energy that HISC-99 can unleash.		 As a key member of the Upwell Consortium, the Outer Ring Excavations (ORE) corporation has been keen to locate and exploit hidden reserves of rare ice containing valuable and rare deposits of Hyper-Isomorphic Strontium Clathrates (HISC). This rare, highly symmetrical, complex yet compact form of Strontium Clathrates is hard to extract and process but has high utility and value in the space industries. Much like standard Strontium Clathrates, HISC can be used to power structure defense systems and forcefields but with greater efficiency and theoretically much greater resistance to incoming damage.

Due to the rarity of the ice variants containing HISC (such as Geodesic Krystallos and Supersymmetrical Gelidus), and the extreme difficulty of processing the dense and molecularly complex ices into useful fuel, ORE has set up special central ice repository and refinery facilities in convenient ice fields. These facilities send out ice mining expeditions to seek more of the rare, fleeting fields of ice that contain the HISC-bearing ice variants and bring the raw materials back to the Ice Refinery for processing into the highly useful and extremely valuable HISC-99 fuel. To attain 99% purity, the raw HISC ices are cracked and refined in a special facility that pumps the high-value HISC-99 into special storage tanks.

The Ice Refinery controls a number of special Automated HISC-99 Tankers which ferry the refined fuel from the refinery to a remote spaceship loading dock under strict computer control. This safety precaution is designed to prevent any accidents involving spaceships that might lead to the catastrophic liberation of the tremendous amounts of energy that HISC-99 can unleash.
